ng-star-inserted"><!----><!----><h3 class="bwc-typo-headline-s ng-star-inserted" id="nombre-bagage-cabine"><rjf-title class="bw-rjf-title"><span>What is my baggage allowance?<!----></span></rjf-title></h3><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></rjf-heading><rjf-paragraph class="bw-rjf-paragraph ng-star-inserted"><p class="bwc-typo-body-m-regular">Your hand baggage allowance and weight restrictions depend on the cabin in which you are traveling.<!----></p></rjf-paragraph><rjf-information-list class="bw-rjf-information-list ng-star-inserted"><ul class="ng-star-inserted"><rjf-recursive-list class="ng-star-inserted"><li>In the Economy cabin, you may take 1 hand baggage and 1&nbsp;personal item.<!----><!----></li></rjf-recursive-list><rjf-recursive-list class="ng-star-inserted"><li>If you are traveling in the Premium Economy, Business, or La&nbsp;Première cabin, you may take 2&nbsp;hand baggage items and 1&nbsp;personal item.<!----><!----></li></rjf-recursive-list><!----></ul><!----><!----><!----><!----></rjf-information-list><rjf-paragraph class="bw-rjf-paragraph ng-star-inserted"><p class="bwc-typo-body-m-regular">Hand baggage on flights to the United States is subject to U.S. regulations and the Transportation Security Administration (TSA).<!----></p></rjf-paragraph><!----></div><!----><!----></div></bw-information-section-template><bw-information-section-template class="bw-information-section bw-information-section--full-width ng-star-inserted"><div class="bw-information-section__grid-container bw-information-section__image--right"><div class="bw-information-section__content-container"><rjf-heading class="bw-rjf-heading ng-star-inserted"><!----><!----><h3 class="bwc-typo-headline-s ng-star-inserted" id="dimensions"><rjf-title class="bw-rjf-title"><span>Hand baggage dimensions<!----></span></rjf-title></h3><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></rjf-heading><rjf-paragraph class="bw-rjf-paragraph ng-star-inserted"><p class="bwc-typo-body-m-regular">The maximum dimensions of your hand baggage are: 55&nbsp;x&nbsp;35&nbsp;x&nbsp;25&nbsp;cm/21.7 x 13.8 x 9.9 in. (including pockets, wheels, and handles).

Not sure if your bag meets these dimension requirements? Air&nbsp;France offers a range of tools for you to check your baggage dimensions. You will find them at the airport, baggage drop-off areas, and in check-in halls. Baggage checks will be enforced prior to boarding. If your hand baggage does not meet these criteria, you will be asked to place it in the hold. You may incur additional fees.<!----></p></rjf-paragraph><!----></div><div class="bw-information-section__image-container ng-star-inserted"><bwc-content-image bwdeferload="setImageSource" class="bw-information-section__image" _nghost-server-app-c1853638857=""><img _ngcontent-server-app-c1853638857="" loading="lazy" class="bwc-content-image" alt="dimensions-cabin" src="https://img.static-af.com/images/media/BFF87B95-CA12-4E1A-A261F254D2C12E4F?w=480&amp;aspect_ratio=2:1" srcset="https://img.static-af.com/images/media/BFF87B95-CA12-4E1A-A261F254D2C12E4F?w=180&amp;aspect_ratio=2:1 360w, https://img.static-af.com/images/media/BFF87B95-CA12-4E1A-A261F254D2C12E4F?w=300&amp;aspect_ratio=2:1 600w, https://img.static-af.com/images/media/BFF87B95-CA12-4E1A-A261F254D2C12E4F?w=384&amp;aspect_ratio=2:1 768w, https://img.static-af.com/images/media/BFF87B95-CA12-4E1A-A261F254D2C12E4F?w=480&amp;aspect_ratio=2:1 960w" style="aspect-ratio: 2 / 1;"><!----></bwc-content-image></div><!----><!----></div></bw-information-section-template><bw-information-section-template class="bw-information-section bw-information-section--full-width ng-star-inserted"><div class=""><div class="bw-information-section__content-container"><rjf-heading class="bw-rjf-heading ng-star-inserted"><!----><!----><h3 class="bwc-typo-headline-s ng-star-inserted" id="poids"><rjf-title class="bw-rjf-title"><span>Your hand baggage weight<!----></span></rjf-title></h3><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></rjf-heading><rjf-paragraph class="bw-rjf-paragraph ng-star-inserted"><p class="bwc-typo-body-m-regular">In the Economy or Premium Economy cabins, your hand baggage and personal items can weigh up to 12 kg (26.4 lb) in total.

If you are traveling in the Business cabin or in La Première, your hand baggage and personal items can weigh up to 18 kg (40 lb) in total. Your cabin is shown on your ticket.<!----></p></rjf-paragraph><!----></div><!----><!----></div></bw-information-section-template><bw-information-highlight-template class="bw-information-section bw-information-highlight-template__full-width ng-star-inserted"><bwc-highlight-block class="bw-information-highlight-template__block bwc-highlight-block" _nghost-server-app-c3559140530=""><section _ngcontent-server-app-c3559140530=""><!----><bw-information-section-template class="bw-information-section bw-information-section--full-width"><div class=""><div class="bw-information-section__content-container"><rjf-paragraph class="bw-rjf-paragraph ng-star-inserted"><p class="bwc-typo-body-m-regular">Have you chosen a Light fare? Check your text messages and emails&nbsp;!
 If your flight is scheduled to be full or depending on the type of aircraft, we may ask you to check in your hand baggage, free of charge. Please keep all your personal belongings and valuables with you (travel documents, medical paperwork, electronic devices, etc.). 

 We may ask you to check in your hand baggage, free of charge.<!----></p></rjf-paragraph><!----></div><!----><!----></div></bw-information-section-template></section></bwc-highlight-block></bw-information-highlight-template><bw-information-section-template class="bw-information-section bw-information-section--full-width ng-star-inserted"><div class="bw-information-section__grid-container bw-information-section__image--right"><div class="bw-information-section__content-container"><rjf-heading class="bw-rjf-heading ng-star-inserted"><!----><!----><h3 class="bwc-typo-headline-s ng-star-inserted" id="accessoires"><rjf-title class="bw-rjf-title"><span>Authorized personal items<!----></span></rjf-title></h3><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></rjf-heading><rjf-paragraph class="bw-rjf-paragraph ng-star-inserted"><p class="bwc-typo-body-m-regular">Soft plastic bags and packaging made with rudimentary means (e.g., household stretch film) are not accepted.
Such package damages airport facilities and disrupts baggage transit.

 Any baggage that is visibly damaged, poorly packed, or not in compliance will be refused.<!----></p></rjf-paragraph><!----></div><div class="bw-information-section__image-container class="bw-rjf-title"><span>Additional items you may take on board...<!----></span></rjf-title></h3><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></rjf-heading><rjf-paragraph class="bw-rjf-paragraph ng-star-inserted"><p class="bwc-typo-body-m-regular"><rjf-plain-text class="ng-star-inserted">The following items are neither considered a personal item nor hand baggage, and can be brought on board:
- jacket, coat, or any other item of clothing you may be wearing
- umbrella,
- duty-free items that you purchased on board or at the airport,
- children's accesories, including strollers*, car seats, diaper bags (please visit our&nbsp;<!----></rjf-plain-text><rjf-link class="ng-star-inserted"><!----><a class="" href="/information/passagers/familles-enfants">Families and children</a><!----></rjf-link><rjf-plain-text class="ng-star-inserted">&nbsp;page),

<span class="bw-information-italic">*&nbsp;Depending on available space on board. Should there not be enough space on board for your stroller, we will put it in the hold, free of charge.</span><!----></rjf-plain-text><!----></p></rjf-paragraph><!----></div><!----><!----></div></bw-information-section-template></section></bwc-highlight-block></bw-information-highlight-template><bw-information-section-template class="bw-information-section bw-information-section--full-width ng-star-inserted"><div class="bw-information-section__grid-container bw-information-section__image--right"><div class="bw-information-section__content-container"><rjf-heading class="bw-rjf-heading ng-star-inserted"><!----><!----><h3 class="bwc-typo-headline-s ng-star-inserted" id="produit-ok-cabine"><rjf-title class="bw-rjf-title"><span>Authorized items in the cabin<!----></span></rjf-title></h3><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></rjf-heading><rjf-paragraph class="bw-rjf-paragraph ng-star-inserted"><p class="bwc-typo-body-m-regular">You can carry liquids, pastes, and creams in the cabin under the following conditions:
<!----></p></rjf-paragraph><rjf-information-list class="bw-rjf-information-list ng-star-inserted"><ul class="ng-star-inserted"><rjf-recursive-list class="ng-star-inserted"><li>containers must be placed in a transparent and closed plastic bag,<!----><!----></li></rjf-recursive-list><rjf-recursive-list class="ng-star-inserted"><li>each container cannot exceed 100&nbsp;ml / 3.4 oz.<!----><!----></li></rjf-recursive-list><rjf-recursive-list class="ng-star-inserted"><li>your plastic bag cannot exceed 1 liter.<!----><!----></li></rjf-recursive-list><rjf-recursive-list class="ng-star-inserted"><li>the plastic bag cannot be bigger than 20&nbsp;x&nbsp;20&nbsp;cm/7.8 x 7.8 in.<!----><!----></li></rjf-recursive-list><!----></ul><!----><!----><!----><!----></rjf-information-list><rjf-paragraph class="bw-rjf-paragraph ng-star-inserted"><p class="bwc-typo-body-m-regular"><rjf-plain-text class="ng-star-inserted">
 Please note: only 1 plastic bag per passenger is allowed. 
Some liquids are allowed on board with no restrictions (baby food, medication, etc.). class="bwc-typo-body-m-regular">You can declare a missing baggage item by filling out the form below, or via the Air&nbsp;France app within 48 &nbsp;hours of your flight's arrival. To do so, please locate your baggage receipt. 

Where can you find my baggage receipt?&nbsp;
- If you checked in at the airport, your receipt was given &nbsp;to you by &nbsp;one of our agents at the drop-off area.
- If you printed out your baggage tags and boarding pass at home, your receipt number will be located on the Baggage &nbsp;Receipt page &nbsp;and on the confirmation email that was sent to you.

Add the receipt number to the online form. You will receive a &nbsp;claim number once you have submitted your request. Keep your claim number close to track the status of your request.

Please note that certain airports do not allow you to declare a missing baggage item online.<!----></p></rjf-paragraph><!----></div><!----><div class="bw-information-section__subsection-container ng-tns-c857250080-20"><div class="ng-tns-c857250080-20"><div class="bw-information-section__content-container"><bw-information-section-template class="bw-information-section"><div class=""><div class="bw-information-section__content-container"><rjf-paragraph class="bw-rjf-paragraph ng-star-inserted" style=""><p class="bwc-typo-body-m-regular"><rjf-plain-text class="ng-star-inserted">We kindly ask you to complete the inventory and claim form available after identification in the <!----></rjf-plain-text><rjf-link class="ng-star-inserted"><a class="bwc-o-link-ext" href="https://wtrweb.worldtracer.aero/WorldTracerWeb/pax.do?airlineCode=AF&amp;siteLanguage=FR" aria-label="online baggage search Opens in new window" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">online baggage search</a><!----><!----></rjf-link><rjf-plain-text class="ng-star-inserted">tool. 
Please include as much detail possible regarding the contents of your missing baggage, including the value of each clothing item, pair of shoes, object, etc.
 The more detail you provide, the better we will be able to locate and identify your baggage. 

If your baggage has not been found within 21 days of &nbsp;your request, the items you have inventoried will serve as the basis of your compensation.*&nbsp;
 If you can produce receipts (invoices, proof of purchase), your allowance can be as much as €1,607 (the maximum amount set by the Montreal convention). 

<span class="bwc-typo-body-m-bold">Please note</span>&nbsp;: when you check in your baggage, you can purchase additional insurance that allows you to declare the actual value of your belongings, if this is estimated to be higher than the maximum compensation the Montreal Convention provides (€1,607*). Therefore, the refund will be calculated according to the declared value if your baggage is lost. 

<sub><span class="bw-information-italic">* Compensation is expressed in Special Drawing Rights (SDRs), the unit of account of the International&nbsp;Monetary&nbsp;Fund (IMF)&nbsp;: 1&nbsp;288&nbsp;SDR equals approximately €1,&nbsp;607&nbsp;. This amount is subject to currency valuations and is not guaranteed.</span></sub><!----></rjf-plain-text><!----></p></rjf-paragraph><!----></div><!----><!----></div></bw-information-section-template></div><div
